\DoxyCodeLine{00876\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ with\ length\ of\ up\ to\ 23\ chars\ on\ the\ stack\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00877\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ last\ byte\ of\ the\ buffer\ is\ used\ for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00878\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ -\/\ the\ highest\ bit\ -\/\ if\ "{}0"{}\ then\ it\ is\ small\ -\/\ otherwise\ its\ "{}1"{}\ (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00879\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ capacity\ left\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ using\ the\ lowest\ 5\ bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00880\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ 2\ bits\ are\ left\ unused\ -\/\ the\ second\ and\ third\ highest\ ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00881\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ acts\ as\ a\ null\ terminator\ if\ strlen()\ is\ 23\ (24\ including\ the\ null\ terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00882\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ the\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ remains\ "{}0"{}\ ("{}as\ well\ as\ the\ capacity\ left"{})\ so\ its\ OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00883\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Idea\ taken\ from\ this\ lecture\ about\ the\ string\ implementation\ of\ facebook/folly\ -\/\ fbstring}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04106\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS)\ ||\ defined(DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04107\ \textcolor{keyword}{template}\ <\textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{04108\ \textcolor{keyword}{using\ }MultiLaneAtomic\ =\ Atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{04109\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else\ \ }\textcolor{comment}{//\ DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04110\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Provides\ a\ multilane\ implementation\ of\ an\ atomic\ variable\ that\ supports\ add,\ sub,\ load,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04111\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ store.\ Instead\ of\ using\ a\ single\ atomic\ variable,\ this\ splits\ up\ into\ multiple\ ones,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04112\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ each\ sitting\ on\ a\ separate\ cache\ line.\ The\ goal\ is\ to\ provide\ a\ speedup\ when\ most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04113\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ operations\ are\ modifying.\ It\ achieves\ this\ with\ two\ properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04114\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04115\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Multiple\ atomics\ are\ used,\ so\ chance\ of\ congestion\ from\ the\ same\ atomic\ is\ reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04116\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Each\ atomic\ sits\ on\ a\ separate\ cache\ line,\ so\ false\ sharing\ is\ reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04117\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04118\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ disadvantage\ is\ that\ there\ is\ a\ small\ overhead\ due\ to\ the\ use\ of\ TLS,\ and\ load/store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04119\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ slower\ because\ all\ atomics\ have\ to\ be\ accessed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04120\ \textcolor{keyword}{template}\ <\textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{04121\ \textcolor{keyword}{class\ }MultiLaneAtomic\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{04122\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }CacheLineAlignedAtomic\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{04123\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Atomic<T>\ atomic\{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{04124\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ padding[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE\ -\/\ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(Atomic<T>)];}
\DoxyCodeLine{04125\ \ \ \ \ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{04126\ \ \ \ \ CacheLineAlignedAtomic\ m\_atomics[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES];}
\DoxyCodeLine{04127\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{04177\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Each\ thread\ has\ a\ different\ atomic\ that\ it\ operates\ on.\ If\ more\ than\ NumLanes\ threads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04178\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ use\ this,\ some\ will\ use\ the\ same\ atomic.\ So\ performance\ will\ degrade\ a\ bit,\ but\ still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04179\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ everything\ will\ work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04180\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04181\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ logic\ here\ is\ a\ bit\ tricky.\ The\ call\ should\ be\ as\ fast\ as\ possible,\ so\ that\ there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04182\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ is\ minimal\ to\ no\ overhead\ in\ determining\ the\ correct\ atomic\ for\ the\ current\ thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04183\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04184\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 1.\ A\ global\ static\ counter\ laneCounter\ counts\ continuously\ up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04185\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 2.\ Each\ successive\ thread\ will\ use\ modulo\ operation\ of\ that\ counter\ so\ it\ gets\ an\ atomic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04186\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ assigned\ in\ a\ round-\/robin\ fashion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04187\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 3.\ This\ tlsLaneIdx\ is\ stored\ in\ the\ thread\ local\ data,\ so\ it\ is\ directly\ available\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04188\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ little\ overhead.}}
